<span data-ttu-id="ed53f-1063">Esta clase contiene los siguientes atributos para Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ed53f-1063">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
